<p><a href = vnd.unilang:ultimately.html>Ultimately</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Sanskrit" class="extiw" title="w:Sanskrit">Sanskrit</a></span> <i class="Deva mention" lang="sa">तन्त्र</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="sa-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn"><a href = vnd.unilang:tantra.html>tantra</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. <span class="maintenance-line"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:this.html>This</a> etymology <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:incomplete.html>incomplete</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:you.html>You</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:can.html>can</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:help.html>help</a> Wiktionary <a href = vnd.unilang:by.html>by</a> elaborating <a href = vnd.unilang:on.html>on</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:the.html>the</a> origins <a href = vnd.unilang:of.html>of</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:this.html>this</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:term.html>term</a>.</i></span>

***tapas.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:tapas.html>tapas</a> (59033)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>From</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Spanish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Spanish language"><a href = vnd.unilang:spanish.html>Spanish</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="es"><a href = vnd.unilang:tapas.html>tapas</a></i>, plural <a href = vnd.unilang:of.html>of</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="es">tapa</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:with.html>with</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:original.html>original</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:sense.html>sense</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:of.html>of</a> “top”.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun"><a href = vnd.unilang:noun.html>Noun</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:tapas.html>tapas</a></strong> (<i>uncountable</i>)

<p><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">Clipping <a href = vnd.unilang:of.html>of</a> <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Latn mention" lang="en">tarmacadam</i></span></span>, <a href = vnd.unilang:which.html>which</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:tar.html>tar</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">macadam</i> (crushed <a href = vnd.unilang:stones.html>stones</a>). <a href = vnd.unilang:originally.html>Originally</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:a.html>a</a> trademark owned <a href = vnd.unilang:by.html>by</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:its.html>its</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:inventor.html>inventor</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:edgar.html>Edgar</a> Hooley.
